2/21/25, 4:32â€¯PM - Chris Bro: https://www.walkersanderson.com/obituaries/Brent-Theurer?obId=37279176
2/21/25, 5:11â€¯PM - Chris Bro: Many of you may remember President Theurer as our stake President in the Rincon Stake. Above is the link to his obituary. Although I never knew him very well, he was the stake president who interviewed me as I was preparing for my mission. 
I still remember clearly a specific part of that interview where he asked what I would do if I was on my mission and started feeling depressed. I responded that I would pray for Help. He asked what I would do if I was praying harder and still feeling depressed. I gave several more Sunday school answers such as reading my scriptures more, etc. He continued to ask what would I do if I was still feeling depressed after doing all of those things. He was very familiar with the circumstances with our dadâ€˜s mental health, and as I understood, he had also struggled with his own mental health. His point and what he emphasize to me was that if I was trying to do all the right things and was still having struggles with mental health that it was important to seek professional help, including Counseling and or taking medication if needed. Although I was blessed on my mission to not have any challenges with mental health, there was a period a few months after my mission where I did begin to feel significant depression and anxiety. I remembered his counsel and ended up going to see a counselor, as well as started treatment with an antidepressant for about a year that made a huge difference for me at that time.    Although I have not needed prescription medication for depression since then, I will always remember his counsel and would not hesitate to seek help again in the future if it was ever needed. 
I am very grateful to have known President  Theurer. My thoughts and prayers are with his family.
